> #  deleteOne ู deleteMany

> # comparison operators

ุชู ุงู ูุณูุช ุงุฒ ุฏูุชุง ููุจุน https://www.w3schools.com/mongodb/mongodb_query_operators.php ุจุฎุด MongoDB Query Operators 


ู ุณุงุช https://www.mongodbtutorial.org/ ุจุฎุด Comparison Query Operators ฺฉู ุจุฑุง ูุฑฺฉุฏูู ู ูุซุงู ุฒุฏู 
ุฏุฑ ฺฉู ูุฑุงุฑู ุจุง ุงู ุณู ุฏุณุชู ุจูุฏ ฺฉุงููุฏ ูุง mongoshell ุขุดูุง ุจุดู ู ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑุฏ ูุง ุดู ุจุฑุณ ฺฉูู



Comparison
The following operators can be used in queries to compare values:

- $eq: Values are equal
- $ne: Values are not equal
- $gt: Value is greater than another value
- $gte: Value is greater than or equal to another value
- $lt: Value is less than another value
- $lte: Value is less than or equal to another value
- $in: Value is matched within an array
----------



Logical
The following operators can logically compare multiple queries.

- $and: Returns documents where both queries match
- $or: Returns documents where either query matches
- $nor: Returns documents where both queries fail to match
- $not: Returns documents where the query does not match
---------


Evaluation
The following operators assist in evaluating documents.

- $regex: Allows the use of regular expressions when evaluating field values
- $text: Performs a text search
- $where: Uses a JavaScript expression to match documents
--------


ูุฑุถ ฺฉูู ฺฉู ูุง ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณููู ู ฺฉุงูฺฉุดู users ุฏุงุฑู ฺฉู 7 ุชุง ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ุฏุงุฎูุด ูุณุชู:

> # ุงูพุฑุงุชูุฑ-and$


Comparison
The following operators can be used in queries to compare values:

- $eq: Values are equal
- $ne: Values are not equal
- $gt: Value is greater than another value
- $gte: Value is greater than or equal to another value
- $lt: Value is less than another value
- $lte: Value is less than or equal to another value
- $in: Value is matched within an array
----------



Logical
The following operators can logically compare multiple queries.

- $and: Returns documents where both queries match
- $or: Returns documents where either query matches
- $nor: Returns documents where both queries fail to match
- $not: Returns documents where the query does not match
---------


Evaluation
The following operators assist in evaluating documents.

- $regex: Allows the use of regular expressions when evaluating field values
- $text: Performs a text search
- $where: Uses a JavaScript expression to match documents
--------

ุฏุงุฎู ูพูุดู pages ู ูพูุดู api ุฏุงุฑู  ฺฉู ู ูุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู ูุซูุง milad.js ู ุฏุงุฎู index.js ฺฉู ุตูุญู ุงุตู ุง ูููู ุฑูุช ุงุตู ูุณุช ูู ุณู ุชุง ุฏฺฉูู ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู ุจุฑุง ุงููุงุน ุงุฑุณุงู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช ูุงููู

```jsx
// pages>index.js

export default function Home() {

  const getRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/milad' , {method : 'GET'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
    
  }
  const postRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/milad' , {method : 'POST'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }
  const putRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/milad' , {method : 'PUT'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }
  const deleteRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/milad' , {method : 'DELETE'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }

  return (
    <>
      <button onClick={getRequestHandler}>get request</button>
      <button onClick={postRequestHandler}>post request</button>
      <button onClick={putRequestHandler}>put request</button>
      <button onClick={deleteRequestHandler}>delete request</button>
    </>
  );
}

```
```
// pages>api>milad.js

 export default function handler(req , res){
    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        res.json({name : 'milad' , family : 'bahrami'})
    }else if(req.method == 'POST'){
        res.json({message : 'new user added to database'})
    }else if(req.method == 'PUT'){
        res.json({message : 'users update success fully'})
    }else if(req.method == 'DELETE'){
        res.json({message : 'user delete success fully'})
    }
 }
```

> # ุงุฑุณุงู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช ุจุง ูุชุฏ GET

ุชู ุงู ูุณูุช ูุฎูุงู ู ุตูุญู users ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉูู ฺฉู ูุฒุฑูุงูููู ุชู ุงูู ุตูุญู ููุงุด ุจุฏู ู ุจุฑุง  ฺฏุฑูุชู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ูุฒุฑูุงููู ูุชููู ู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช ุจุฒูู ุจู ุงุฏุฑุณ https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users ู ุง ุงุฒ ุงูู ูุงู ฺฉู ุชู ูุณูุช ูุจู ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจูุฏู ฺฉู ฺูุงุฑ ุชุง ูุฒุฑ ุฏุงุดุช ู ุชู ูุงู ูพูุดู pages > api > users > index.js ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจูุฏู ูุชููู ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉูู ฺฉู ุฑูุชุด ูุดุฏ http://localhost:3000/api/users ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉูู .
ุฎุจ ูุง ุงูู ุงููุฏู ู ุฑูุช user ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุชู ูพูุดู pages ู ูพูุดู ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจู ุงุณู users ู ุฏุงุฎูุด ู ูุงู index.js ุณุงุฎุชู ู ุงุณู ฺฉุงููพูููุช ุฑู ฺฏุฒุงุดุชู users

```js
//pages>users>index.js
import UserDetail from "@/components/userdetail"
import styles from '@/styles/user.module.css'
import { useEffect, useState } from "react"


export default function users(){

    const [users , setUser] = useState([])
    const getUsers = async ()=>{
        const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users')
        const data = await res.json()
        setUser(data);
        console.log(data);
        
    }
    useEffect(()=>{
        getUsers()
    } , [])

    return (
        <>
            <h1>All Users</h1>
            {
                users.map((user)=>(
                    <div className={styles.user} key={user.id}>
                        <UserDetail {...user}/>
                    </div>
                    
                ))
            }
           
        </>
    )
} 

```
ุงฺฏู ุฏูุช ฺฉูู ูุง ุชู ูุณูุช fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users',{method : 'GET'}) ู ุฏฺฏู ุชู ูพุงุฑุงูุชุฑ ุฏูู ฺฉู ู ุงุจุฌฺฉุช ูุณุช ููุน ุงุฑุณุงู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช ุฑู ูฺฏูุชู ฺฉู get ูุณุช ฺูู ุจุตูุฑุช ูพุดูุฑุถ ุฎูุฏุด ุจุง method get ุงุฑุณุงู ูุดู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช
ุชู ุฑูุช ุงุตู ู ูพูุดู componets ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ูุฎูุงู ู ฺฉุงููพูููุช ุจู ุงุณู userDetail ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ฺฉู ููุช ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ูุฒุฑูุงุฑู ุงุฒ ุฏุชุงุจุณ ฺฏุฑูุชู ุจุฑุง ูุฑฺฉุฏูู ุงุฒ ูุฒุฑ ูุง ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉูู ูพุณ ุฏุงุฎู ูพูุดู components ู ูุงู userDetail.js ุฏุงุฑู .
```js
//components>userdetail.js

 function UserDetail ({id , name , family , age , email }){
    return(
        <div>
            <p>name : </p><b>{name}</b>
            <p>family : </p><b>{family}</b>
            <p>gamil : </p><b>{email}</b>
            <p>age : </p><b>{age}</b>
        </div>
    )
}
export default UserDetail
```

ูููฺูู ุงูู ูุงู ฺฉู ุณุงุฎุชู ุจูุฏู ุชู ูพูุดู api ุฎูุฏููู ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจูุฏู ู ุฏุชุงุจุณ ุฑู . ุฏุงุฎู ูพูุดู pages , ูพูุดู api ู ูพูุดู ุฏุงุฑู ุจู ุงุณู user ู ุฏุงุฎู ุงูู index.js

```js
//pages>api>users>index.js
const users = [

    {
        id: 1,

        age: 19,

      },

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        res.json(users)
    }
}
```

> # dynamic api route

ูุจูุง ุจุง ุฑูุช ูุง ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ dynamic route ุงุดูุง ุดุฏู ูุงูุง ูุฎูุงู ุจุจูู ุชู ูููุฏุฑ api ฺุทูุฑ ูุชููู ุฑูุช ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ุทุฑูู ฺฉุงุฑ ูุซู ูููู ุฑูุช ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ ูุณุช .ูุง ุชู ูุณูุช ูุจู ุฏุงุฎู ูููุฏุฑ pages ู ูููุฏุฑ api ูุณุช ฺฉู ุฏุงูุฎุด ูุง ู ูููุฏุฑ users ู ุฏุงุฎูุด ู ูุงู index.js ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจูุฏู ฺฉู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ููู ูุฒุฑ ูุง ุฑู ุฏุงุดุชู ู ุฌูุฑุง ฺฉุงูฺฉุดู users ุชู mongodb ุฑู ุดุจู ุณุงุฒ ฺฉุฑุฏู ุจูุฏู ู ุงฺฏู ู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช GET ูุฒุฏู ุจู ุงู ุงูู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฑู ุฏุฑูุงูุจ ุฑุดุชู json ุจูููู ูุฏุงุฏ ฺฉู ุฑูุชุด ุงู ูุณุช localhost:3000/api/users ููุง ูุฎูุงู ู ุฑูุช ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ api ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉูู ูุงู ฺฉูุงุฑ ููู index.js ฺฉู ุฏุงุฎู ูููุฏุฑ users ูุณุช ู ูุงู js[userId]. ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู ูุฎูุงู ูุซูุง ุงฺฏู ุฒุฏู localhost:3000/api/users/1 ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุงูู ูุฒุฑ ุงูู ุฑู ุจฺฏุฑู ูุซู ุงูู api ูฺฉ ุณุงุช jsonplasholder ฺฉู ููุช ูุฒุฏ ุงุฎุฑ ุงุฏุฑุณุด 1/users... ุง 2/users... ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุงูู ูุฒุฑ ุฑู ูุฏุงุฏ ุฏุฑูุงูุน ูุฑู ู ุงูู ูุฒุฑ ฺฉู ูุซูุง ุงุฏุด 1 ูุณุช ุฑู ูุฏู ุงุงูู ุฑู ูพุฏุง ูฺฉูู ุฏฺฏู ููู ูุฒุฑูุง ุฑู ููุฏู. ูุง ูู ูุฎูุงู ููู ฺฉุงุฑู ฺฉูู ุฑูุช ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ api ุชูุณุนู ุจุฏู

```js
//pages>api>users>[userId].js

const users = [

    {
        id: 1,
        name: "milad",
        family: "bahrami",
        email: "milad@yahoo.com",
        password: "12345678m",
        age: 24,
        gender: "male"
      },
      {
        id : 2,
        name: "ali",
        family: "karimi",
        email: "ali@yahoo.com",
        password: "12345678a",
        age: 24,
        gender: "male"
      },
      {
        id : 3,
        name: "nika",
        family: "shahkarami",
        email: "nika@yahoo.com",
        password: "12345678n",
        age: 21,
        gender: "female"
      },
      {
        id : 4,
        name: "asghar",
        family: "ahmadi",
        email: "asghar@yahoo.com",
        password: "12345678as",
        age: 19,
        gender: "male"
      },

]

export default function handler(req , res){
    const {userId} = req.query
    const user = users.find((userItem)=> userItem.id == userId)
    console.log(user);
    
    if(user){
        res.json(user)
    }else{
        res.json({massage : 'user not found'})
    }
    
}

```

```js
const users = [

    {
        id: 1,
        name: "milad",

export default function handler(req , res){
    const {userId} = req.query
    const user = users.find((userItem)=> userItem.id == userId)
    console.log(user);
    
    if(user){
	//ุฑูุด ุงูู
	res.statusCode = 200
        res.json(user)
    }else{
	//ุฑูุด ุฏูู
        res.status(404).json({massage : 'user not found'})
    }
    
}
```

ุงูุงู ุงฺฏู ูุง ูุงุฑุฏ ุฑูุช localhost:3000/api/users/1 ุจุดู ู ุงุฒ ุตูุญู inspect ุจฺฏุฑู ู ูุงุฑุฏ ุชุจ Network ุจุดู ู ุฑู ุงู ูุงู ฺฉูฺฉ ฺฉูู ูุจูู ฺฉู ููุดุชู status code : 200 ok ุงูุง ุงฺฏู ูุงุฑุฏ ุฑูุช localhost:3000/api/users/20 ุจุดู ฺูู ูุง 4 ุชุง ูุฒุฑ ุฏุงุฑู ู ุงู ูุฒุฑ ุฑู ูุฏุงุฑู ูููุณู status code : 404 notFound

ูุจ ุจุฑู ฺฉู ุงุฒ ุณูุช ูุฑุงูุช ู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช post ุจุฒูู ู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฑู ุชู request body ุงุฑุณุงู ฺฉูู ุจู api . ุฎุจ ูุง ู ุฏฺฉูู ุฏฺฏู ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู ุจุฑุง ุงูฺฉุงุฑ ฺฉู ุงุณูุดู send user body ฺฏุฒุงุดุชู ุชู ูุณูุช ูุง ูุจู ุฏุงุฎู ุตูุญู ุงุตู ูุจ ุณุงุชููู ุฑูุช ุงุตู index.js ฺูุงุฑ ุชุง ุฏฺฉูู ุฏุงุดุชู ู ุฏฺฉูู ุฏฺฏู ูู ุจุฑุง ุงูฺฉุงุฑ ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู ฺฉู ุจุง ูุชุฏ POST ูุฎูุงู requst ุจุฒูู ุจู ุณุฑูุฑ ุจุง api 

ูพุณ ูุง ูุฎูุงู ู ุฏฺฉูู ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ฺฉู ููุช ุฑู ุงูู ฺฉูฺฉ ูุดู ุงุฒ ุณูุช ูุฑูุฑฺฏุฑ ู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช ูุฑุณุชุงุฏู ุจุดู ุจู ุณูุช ุณุฑูุฑ ูุชู ุจุฏูู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช ุจุงู ู ุณุฑ ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฑู ุจูุฑุณุชู ุจู ุณูุช ุณุฑูุฑ ู ุฏุฑููุงุช ุจู respons ูุชูุงุณุจ ูู ุฏุฑุงูุช ฺฉูู 

```js
// index.js
// localhost:300 ุงู ูุงู ุฑูุช ุงุตู ูุณุช  ุตูุญู ุงุตู


export default function Home() {
 

  const getRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users' , {method : 'GET'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
    
  }
  const postRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users' , {method : 'POST'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }
  const putRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users' , {method : 'PUT'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }
  const deleteRequestHandler = async ()=>{
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users' , {method : 'DELETE'})
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
  }
  const sendUserBody = async ()=> {
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users',{
        method : 'POST',
        body : JSON.stringify(
          {
            name : 'reza',
            family : 'bahrami',
            email : 'rezabahrami@gamil.com',
            password : '14445d',
            age : 21,
            gender : 'male'
          }
        ),
        headers :{
          'Content-Type' : 'application/json'
        }
      })
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
    
  }

  return (
    <>
      <button onClick={getRequestHandler}>get request</button>
      <button onClick={postRequestHandler}>post request</button>
      <button onClick={putRequestHandler}>put request</button>
      <button onClick={deleteRequestHandler}>delete request</button>
      <button onClick={sendUserBody}>send user body</button>
    </>
  );
}
```

ุชู ูุณูุช ูุจู ู ุฏฺฉูู send user body  ุฏุงุดุชู ฺฉู ููุช ุฑูุด ฺฉูฺฉ ูฺฉุฑุฏู ฺฉุฏ ูุง ูุงูฺฉุดู sendUserBody ุงุฌุฑุง ูุดุฏ ฺฉู ู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช POST ู ุจุง body ุฑู ูู ุฎูุฏููู ฺฉู ู ุงุจุฌฺฉุช ุจุง ุฑุดุชู json ฺฉู ุฎูุฏููู ููุดุชู ุจูุฏู ูุฑุณุชุงุฏู ูุดุฏ request ูุดุฏ ุจู ุณูุช ุจฺฉูุฏ ู ุงููุฌุง ุจู ุงู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฏุณุชุฑุณ ุฏุงุดุชู ุชูุณุท req.body ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ฺฉู ุชู request body ุงุฑุณุงู ฺฉุฑุฏู ุฑู ูุชููู ุณูุช ุจฺฉูุฏ ุฏุฑุงูุช ฺฉูู ู ุจุนุฏ ุงู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฑู ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณ ุซุจุช ูฺฉูู ุชู ุงู ูุณูุช ูุฎูุงู ุจุฌุง ุงูฺฉู ุฎูุฏููู ุจููุณู ุจุตูุฑุช ุฏุณุช  ฺูุฏ input ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ฺฉู ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑ ููุช ุงููุง ุฑู ูพุฑ ูฺฉูู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ฺฏุฑูุชู ุจุดู ู ุจุฑู ุณูุช ุฏุชุงุจุณ  ูุง ุฏุงุฑู ุฏุฑุจุงูุช ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฑู ฺฉุงุฑ ูฺฉูู ุซุจุช ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณ ู ุงุฑุชุจุงุท ูฺฉุณุช ุฌ ุงุณ ุจุง mongodb ุฑู ุชู ูุตู ุงูุฏู ุจุฑุณ ูฺฉูู.

```js
//pages>index.js
import styles from '@/styles/Home.module.css'
import { useState } from "react";

export default function Home() {
 
  const [name , setName] = useState('')
  const [family , setFamily] = useState('')
  const [email , setEmail] = useState('')
  const [password , setPassword] = useState('')
  const [age , setAge] = useState('')
 
  const sendRequestHandler = async ()=> {
    const res = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/users',{
        method : 'POST',
        body : JSON.stringify(
          {
//ูุฏููู ฺฉู ุชู ES6 ุชู ุงุจุฌฺฉุช ุงฺฏู ูพุฑุงูพุฑุช ู ููู ูููุงู ุจุงุดู ูุชููู ฺฉ ุดููู ุจููุณู
            name ,
            family ,
            email,
            password,
	    age
          }
        ),
        headers :{
          'Content-Type' : 'application/json'
        }
      })
    const data = await res.json()
    console.log(data);
    
  }

  return (
    <>
    <div className={styles.form}>
      <input type="text" placeholder='name' value={name} onChange={(e)=>{setName(e.target.value)}} />
      <input type="text" placeholder='family' value={family} onChange={(e)=>{setFamily(e.target.value)}} />
      <input type="email" placeholder='email' value={email} onChange={(e)=>{setEmail(e.target.value)}} />
      <input type="password" placeholder='password' value={password} onChange={(e)=>{setPassword(e.target.value)}} />
      <input type="number" placeholder='age' value={age} onChange={(e)=>{setAge(e.target.value)}} />
      <button onClick={sendRequestHandler}>send request</button>
    </div>
    </>
  );
}
```

ุงูุงู ููุช ุฑู ุฏฺฉูู send request ฺฉูฺฉ ูุดู ุงุทูุงุนุงุช ุฏุงุฎู input ูุง ุชู state ูุง ฺฉู ููุดุชู ุฏุฑููุงุช ู ุงุจุฌฺฉุช ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู ุฐุฎุฑู ูุดู ู ูุฑุณุชุงุฏู ูุดู ุจู ุณูุช ุจฺฉูุฏ ูุง ุงููุฏู ุจู ุงุฒุง ูุฑฺฉุฏูู ุงุฒ input ูุง ู state ููุดุชู ุงูุจุชู ุฑูุด ูุง ุฏฺฏู ุง ูู ุฏุงุฑู ฺฉู ูุชููุณุชู ููุท ุจุง ู state ุงู ฺฉุงุฑู ุจฺฉูู

```js
    console.log(name);//ุงูู ุณูุช ุชุฑููุงู ูุดูู ูุฏู
```

> # mime type|Context-Type

```js
    console.log(data);
```

```js
//pages>api>catacts>index.js

import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db/contact')       //=> uri/databaseName/collectionName
    .then(()=> {console.log('conected database');
    })
    .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    })

    res.json({massage : 'conecte to db succesfully'})
}
```

```js
//models>contact.js

import { models , model , schema } from "mongoose";

const contactSchema = new schema({
    name : {
        type : String
       // minLength : 4 => ูุซูุง ูุชููู ุจฺฏู ุญุฏุงูู 4 ุชุง ุญุฑู ุจุงุฏ ุจุดู ุงูุจุชู ุงูู ูููุดุชู ฺฉู ุณุงุฏู ุชุฑ ููุดุชู ุงูุง ุฑู ูุดุฎุต ูฺฉุฑุฏู
    },
    family : {
        type : String
    },
    age :{
        type : String
    },
    phone : {
        type : String
    },
    gender : {
        type : String
    }

})

const Contact = model('contact' , contactSchema)
export default Contact
```

ุฏุงุฎู ุงู ูุง ุจุงุฏ ุณู ุชุง ฺุฒ ุฑู ุงุฒ mongoose inport ฺฉูู ฺฉู model , models , schmea ูุณุชู ุงุฒ ุงู ูพฺฉุฌ ฺฏุฑูุชู ุจุนุง ู schema ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู schema ุจู ูุนู ุทุฑุญ ,ุงูฺฏู ู ููฺู ฺุฒ ูุณุช ูุง ุจุงุฏ ุจุงู ุทุฑุญ ู ุงูฺฏู ู ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑ ุงู ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ูุง ฺฉู ูุฑุงุฑ ุฏุงุฎู ฺฉุงูฺฉุดู contacts ุซุจุช ุจุดู ุฑู ูุดุฎุต ฺฉูู ุจุง ุฏุฑุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู schema  ููุง ูุซูุง ฺฏูุชู ฺฉู ูุฑ ฺฉุฏูู ุงุฒ ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ูุง ูพุฑุงูพุฑุช name ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ู ููุน ุงูู ุฑุดุชู ุจุงุดู ุนู ุชู ุงู name ุจุงุฏ ฺู ููุน ุฐุฎุฑู ุจุดู `ุงูุจุชู ุฌููุชุฑ ุจู ู ุงุฑูุฑ ูุฎูุฑู ฺฉู ุจุนุฏุง ุจุฑุณุด ูฺฉูู `

```js
      .connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
      .then(() => console.log("connect to db successfully"))
      .catch((error) => console.log(error))

   if (req.method == "GET") {
      const contacts = await Contact.find()      
      res.json(contacts)
   }
}

```

ุจุฑุง ุฑูุน ุงู ุงุฑูุฑ ุชู ูุงู models>contacts.js ุฑู ฺฉู ุฌูุณู ูุจู ููุดุชู ุจูุฏู ุฑู ุงูุทูุฑ ุจุงุฏ ุจููุณู

```js
//models>contacts.js

import { models , model , Schema } from "mongoose";

const contactSchema = new Schema({
    name : {
        type : String
    },
    family : {
        type : String
    },
    age :{
        type : Number
    },
    phone : {
        type : String
    },
    gender : {
        type : String
    }

})

const Contact = models.contact || model('contact' , contactSchema)
export default Contact
```

> # ุจููู ุชุฑ ฺฉุฑุฏู ฺฉุฏ ุงุชุตุงู ุจู ุฏุชุงุจุณ

```js
//pages>api>contacts>index.js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
   mongoose
      .connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
      .then(() => {
         if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log("connect to db successfully")
         }
      })
      .catch((error) => console.log(error))

   if (req.method == "GET") {
      const contacts = await Contact.find()      
      res.json(contacts)
   }
}
```

ููุช ุฑูุช ุฏุงูุงูฺฉ ูุฎูุงุณุชู ุงุณู ูุงู ุฑู ุฏุงุฎู [] ูุฒุงุดุชู ฺฉู ูุง ุงุณูุดู[id_] ฺฏุฒุงุดุชุณู ูููุงู ุจุง ุงูู ููุฏ id_ ฺฉู ุชู ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ูุฑฺฉุฏูู ุงุฒ ูุฎุงุทุจ ูุง ูุณุช ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณ. 

```js
//pages>api>contacts>[_id]

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    .then(()=>{
        if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
            
        }
    })
    .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    })

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        const {_id} = req.query
        const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
        res.json(contact)
    }
}
```

> # ุงุนุชุจุงุฑุณูุฌ-object-ID

ุชูุณุท ูุชุฏ isValidObjectId ฺฉู ุงุฒ mongoose ูู import ูุดู 

```js
//	pages>api>contacts>[_id].js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    .then(()=>{
        if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
            
        }
    })
    .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    })

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        const {_id} = req.query

        if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            res.json(contact)
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
    }
}

```

```js
//	pages>api>contacts/[_id].js
import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    .then(()=>{
        if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
            
        }
    })
    .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    })

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        const {_id} = req.query

        if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
    }
}

```

ุชู ูุณูุช ุจุนุฏ ฺฉู ฺฉุฏ ุฑู ุจููู ุชุฑ ูฺฉูู ฺูู ูุง ุชู ูุงู api>contacts>index.js ู api>contacts>[_id].js ุงูู ูุณูุช ฺฉู ุฏุงุฑู ุจู ุฏุชุงุจุณ next-db ูุชุตู ูุดู ุชฺฉุฑุงุฑ ูุณุช ู ุงู ฺฉุฏ ุชฺฉุฑุงุฑ ูุณุช ู ุชู ูุณูุช ุจุนุฏ ุจููู ุชุฑุด ูฺฉูู.

ูพุณ ูุง ุงู ุชฺฉู ฺฉุฏ ุจุงูุง ุฑู ุชู ุฏูุชุง ูุงู ุฏุงุฑู 


```js
//	pages>api>contacts/[_id].js
import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    .then(()=>{
        if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
            
        }
    })
    .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    })

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        const {_id} = req.query

        if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
    }
}
```

```js
//	pages>api>contacts>index.js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
   mongoose
      .connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
      .then(() => {
         if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
            return
            console.log("connect to db successfully")
         }
      })
      .catch((error) => console.log(error))

   if (req.method == "GET") {
      const contacts = await Contact.find()      
      res.json(contacts)
   }
}
```

ูุงู ุฎุงุฑุฌ ุงุฒ ูุฑฺฏููู ูููุฏุฑ . ุฎูุฏููู ู ูููุฏุฑ ุจุง ุงุณู utils ุงุฌุงุฏ ูฺฉูู  ุฏุงุฎู ุงู ูููุฏุฑ utils ูุง ูุซูุง ุงฺฏู ฺฉ ูุงูฺฉุดู ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ฺฉู ูุฑุงุฑ ฺูุฏ ุฌุง ูุฎุชูู ุชู ูพุฑูฺู ููู ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุจุดู ูุงู ุชู ุงู ูููุฏุฑ utils ุงูู ุฑู ุชุนุฑู ูฺฉูู. ุฏุงุฎู ูููุฏุฑ utils ู ูุงู ุจู ุงุณู connectDB.js ุฏุฑุณุช ูฺฉูู  ฺฉู ุงูุจุชู ู ุณุฑ ุชุบุฑุงุช ูู ุฏุงุฑุฏู ุงุฒ try , catch ุจุฑุง ููุฏููฺฏ ุงุฑูุฑ ูุง ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู ู ฺูู ุนููุงุช ุงุฒุชุจุงุท ู ุงุชุตุงู ุจู ุฏุชุงุจุณ ู ุนููุงุช ุฒูุงูุจุฑ ูุณุช ุงุฒ async , await ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู

```js
//	utils>connectDB
export default async function connectDB(){
   try {
    if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState) return
    await mongoose.connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
    console.log("connect to db successfully")
    
   } catch (error) {
    console.log('connection faild');
    
   }

}
```
ููุง ุชู ูุงู pages>api>contacts>index.js ุงูุทูุฑ ูููุณู ููุท ุงู ูุงูฺฉุดู connectDB ุฑู ุตุฏุง ูุฒูู ุจุฌุง  ุชฺฉู ฺฉุฏ ุงุฑุชุจุงุท ุจุง ุฏุชุง ุจุณ
```js
//	pages>api>contacts>index.js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
   // mongoose
   //    .connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
   //    .then(() => {
   //       if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
   //          return
   //          console.log("connect to db successfully")
   //       }
   //    })
   //    .catch((error) => console.log(error))

   await connectDB()

   if (req.method == "GET") {
      const contacts = await Contact.find()      
      res.json(contacts)
   }
}
```
ู ููฺูู ุฏุงุฎู ูุงู pages>api>contacts>[_id].js 
```js
//	pages>api>contacts>[_id].js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    // mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    // .then(()=>{
    //     if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
    //         return
    //         console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
    //         
    //     }
    // })
    // .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    // })

    await connectDB()

    if(req.method == 'GET'){
        const {_id} = req.query

        if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
    }
}
```

```js
//	pages>api>contacts.js

import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
   // mongoose
   //    .connect("mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db")
   //    .then(() => {
   //       if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
   //          return
   //          console.log("connect to db successfully")
   //       }
   //    })
   //    .catch((error) => console.log(error))
   await connectDB()

   if (req.method == "GET") {
      const contacts = await Contact.find()      
      res.json(contacts)
   }
   else if(req.method == "POST"){
      
      await Contact.create(req.body)
      res.status(201).json({message : 'new contact added to db'})
      
   }
}
```

> # ุชูุณุนู ูุงุจูุช ุญุฐู ฺฉุฑุฏู ูุฎุงุทุจ

ฺฉ ุฏฺฏู ุงุฒ ูุงุจูุช ูุง ุฏฺฏู ฺฉู ุจุงุฏ ุจุฑูุงูู ูุง ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ุจุชููู ูุฎุงุทุจ ูุง ุฑู ุง ูููู ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ูุง ุฑู ุจุชููู ุงุฒ ฺฉุงูุดู contacts ฺฉู ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณ next-db ูุณุช ุฑู ุจุชููู ุญุฐู ฺฉูู ูุฎูุงู ุงูู ุจู api ููู ุงุถุงูู ฺฉูู .

ุฎุจ ุงูู ุฏุงฺฉูููุช ูุง ฺฉู ุฏุงุฑู ูุฎุงุทุจ ูุง ฺฉู ุฏุงุฑู ุฑู ู ูฺฏุง ุจูุฏุงุฒู ฺฉู ฺูุฏุชุง ูุฎุงุทุจ ุฏุงุฑู ุชู ุฏุชุงุจุณ

ูุงุฑุฏ ูุงู pages>api>contacts>[_id].js  ูุดู ู ู ุณุฑ ุชุบุฑุงุช ูุฏู ู ุงุฒ ูุชุฏ findByIdAndDelete(_id) ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูฺฉูู

```js
//	pages>api>contacts>[_id].js
import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    // mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    // .then(()=>{
    //     if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
    //         return
    //         console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
    //         
    //     }
    // })
    // .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    // })
    await connectDB()
    const {_id} = req.query

    
    if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            if(req.method == 'GET'){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
        }else if(req.method == 'DELETE'){
            await Contact.findByIdAndDelete(_id)
            res.json({message : "contact deleted successfully"})
        }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
}
```
ุชุบุฑุงุช ฺฉู ุฏุงุฑู ุงูู ุชุนุฑู {id_} ุฑู ุจุฑุฏู ุจูุง ฺฉู ุจุชููู ุชู ูุฑ ุฏู ุงุณฺฉููพ ูุง ุดุฑุทูุง GET , DELETE ุจุชููู ุจูุด ุฏุณุชุฑุณ ุฏุงุดุชู ุจุงุดู ุฏุฑ ูุฑุฏูุฌุง ฺูู ูุงุฒุด ุฏุงุฑู ู ููฺูู ุฌุง ุดุฑุท ูุง ุดุฑุท ุงุนุชุจุงุฑ ุณูุฌ ุงุฏ ฺฉู isValidObjectId ูุณุช ุฑู ุจุฑุฏู ุจุงูุงุชุฑ ุงุฒ ุดุฑุท "req.method == "GET ฺู ุจุฑุง ูุฑุฏู ูุงุฒ ุฏุงุฑู ุงุนุชุจุงุฑ ุณูุฌ ุฏุฑุณุช ุจูุฏู ุงุฏ ฺฉู ูุงุฑุฏ ูุดู ุฑู ูุงุฒ ุฏุงุฑู ุจุฑุง ูุฑุฏู ู ุฏุฑููุงุช ุจุฑุง ุญุฐู ฺฉุฑุฏู ุงู ุงุฏ ฺฉู ูุงุฑุฏ ูุดู ุงุฒ ูุชุฏ .findByIdAndDelete(_id) ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู

```js
//	pages>api>contacts>[_id].js
import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    // mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    // .then(()=>{
    //     if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
    //         return
    //         console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
    //         
    //     }
    // })
    // .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    // })
    await connectDB()
    const {_id} = req.query

    
    if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            if(req.method == 'GET'){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
        }else if(req.method == 'DELETE'){
            const result = await Contact.findByIdAndDelete(_id)
            console.log(result);
            
            res.json({message : "contact deleted successfully"})
        }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
}
```

```js
//	pages>api>contacts>[_id].js
import Contact from "@/models/contact";
import connectDB from "@/utils/connectDB";
import mongoose, { isValidObjectId } from "mongoose";

export default async function handler(req , res){
    // mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/next-db')
    // .then(()=>{
    //     if(mongoose.connections[0].readyState){
    //         return
    //         console.log('get contacts to database successfully');
    //         
    //     }
    // })
    // .catch((error)=>{console.log(error);
    // })
    await connectDB()
    const {_id} = req.query

    
    if(isValidObjectId(_id)){
            if(req.method == 'GET'){
            const contact = await Contact.findById(_id)
            if(contact){

                res.json(contact)
            }else{
                res.json({message : 'objectId not found'})
            }
        }else if(req.method == 'DELETE'){
            const result = await Contact.findByIdAndDelete(_id)
            if(result){
                
                res.json({message : "contact deleted successfully"})
            }else{
                res.json({message : "contact not found"})
            }
            
        }
            
        }else{
            res.json({message : 'objectId not value'})
        }
}
```
ุงฺฏู ุงู reult ูุซูุง ุงูุงู ฺุฒ ุชูุด ูุณุช ู ุงุจุฌฺฉุช ุชูุด ูุณุช ุฎุงู ูุณุช ุจุฑุงุจุฑ true ูุณุช ู ุงฺฏู null ุจูุฏ ุจุฑุงุจุฑ faluse ูุณุช . ุงูุงู ุงฺฏู ู ุฏุฑุฎุงุณุช ุจุฒูู ุจู ุงุฏุฑุณ ู ูููู ุงุฏ ฺฉู ุฌุฐู ุดุฏู ูพุบุงู ููุงุณุจ ูุฏู ูฺฏู `{message : "contaact not found"}`
